Listen, as someone that totally gets what she's saying. Someone that can't express myself in that way because if I did it would be racism (even though I've been with a black man for almost two decades and honestly that's all I like is black men lol look white but Italian American in Spanish either way)  She literally laid it all out there, and I f****** love her! Like I said everything that so many of us women can't say, because it would not be right, she did it for us. And I got told by my husband (won't go into detail but let's just say that I have really dealt with some s*** that no good woman should ever have to deal with, and I'm tired of it) that I can't listen to that song, if I do basically I'm a racist. And then he tried to push my buttons and said I bet you want to sing the word. And I said nope I'm just grateful she's putting it out there, cuz it's exactly how I feel.  And then he kept saying ...say it I know you say it, say it.... Now if that isn't gaslighting I don't know what is.  So I never heard this song, but our 16 year old daughter wanted me to hear it, because she felt like it was something that i, as her mother needed to hear.  And my daughter is so wise, wiser  than anybody that I know because I definitely needed to hear this song.   I will continue to play the song, I will listen to it every damn day, because I deserve so much more, and so much better. I don't deserve to be abused in any type of way, I don't deserve to be alienated, to feel completely alone and unloved. I don't deserve to be a secondary to everything when I put everybody else first.  Anyways, sorry for all the blabbering! The song, it literally just pulled me out of a serious depression. A place where I hate going, but go often when I'm treated so damn horribly. Let's just say, something my grandma would say, it's giving me a pep in my step!
